The hotel focuses on the theme of giraffes, which is quite interesting. There are 7 in total, 6 big and 1 small, all very docile. They will not come out when it rains or it is cold. They will get off work on time at 16:00 in the afternoon. Everyone should pay attention to arrange the interaction time. The giraffes will be in the restaurant from 7 to 10 o'clock during breakfast time, but you still have to buy branches üåø arranged by the hotel to lure them over. It costs 30 yuan a handful, the quantity is not large, and it will be gone soon. No food can be brought in to feed them

After arriving at the hotel at noon, check in, and the front desk will skillfully introduce the rules of the hotel. The room supply is tight on weekends, and there is no birthday decoration. After adding the butler v, I kept sending messages enthusiastically and reminded them in various ways, but I never showed up from beginning to end. Do you want to control the number of baths and the number of people? Do you feel sorry for the water?

It was the first little surprise. Then the shuttle bus took the guests staying in the same area to the room. It can be said that the scenery along the way is really beautiful, very natural, very diverse, and there are surprises everywhere. Sometimes it is the Crane Island, sometimes it is a lawn, sometimes it is a giraffe stroll, and sometimes it is a small bridge and flowing water. There are scenes everywhere, but they are not abrupt, and they are integrated with the mountains. I kept wowing along the way, and I couldn't wait to put my luggage away and take a walk. This is the second big surprise. Because I stayed in a light luxury single-family king-size bed room, the guest rooms are one by one hidden in the bamboo forest halfway up the mountain. I have to carry the box and climb some steps, but they are not high, less than 50 steps. Seeing the guest room was another wow~, the third unexpected surprise. Pushing the door in, the small terrace faces the bamboo forest, listening to the wind at night and the birds in the morning, it's so comfortable! The room is also very large, the bed is very comfortable, with double basins, and the air conditioner is already turned on when entering the room, instantly cooling off. Then I couldn't wait to go out for a walk. I added the housekeeper's WeChat, the service attitude was very good, the response speed was very fast, and the shuttle bus was also very fast. But we chose to walk first and get familiar with the manor by ourselves. It's too big, there are too many surprises, and for the first time I felt that there was not enough time. Although the zoo covers a small area, there are not few animals, and they interact happily. The white peacock opened its tail silently beside me! Feeding apples to Crispy Noodles, Crispy Noodles looks really cute. There is also a beautiful little monkey who is not afraid of people. He jumped around us and took a lot of high-definition photos of his face. Then my son played archery, jungle leap, and jungle slide. It was very safe, there were not many people, and the staff were very friendly, but the price was not cheap, and there was no discount for guests staying in the hotel.
It doesn't matter if you don't sit by the window for breakfast. You can stand by the window with a branch to feed the giraffes, because the window seats are 90 cm away from the window, which is specially for children to feed the giraffes, so you don't have to get up early to reserve a seat.
In short, it was a very, very good parent-child trip. The service, environment, and hygiene were all very good. Two days are not enough, I want to go again next time.

After asking the housekeeper, he said that there is only toilet water. It is recommended that mosquito repellent toilet water be provided in the room for customers to use. In Kaiyuan Senbo, each room is provided with a new bottle of toilet water. I hope you can learn from it.
We had two single beds, but we had two children, so we put the two beds together, and then we found biscuits under the bed. These were not the biscuits we brought, so they should have been left by the previous customer.
The shower room and toilet are two separate rooms, but the glass door is completely transparent, and the toilet seat faces the shower room, which is a bit awkward. It would be much better if the direction is changed or the glass is frosted. By the way, the toilet door cannot be pushed inward, as it will hit the toilet. It is recommended that there be a warning on the door.
The service attitude of the housekeeper is still good, and he can basically reply immediately. However, the attitude of other service staff was average and they did not have the enthusiasm of a family hotel. Some shuttle buses would not take the initiative to stop and ask if they wanted a ride when they saw people. We waited at the door and he drove over silently.
The children were given gifts when they left the store, which made them very happy. There are not many activities in the hotel. A giraffe, a cute pet paradise, an insectarium + herbarium are almost over. Everything else basically has to be paid separately.

msg:üìçDingjia Village, Miaoshan Village, Miaoxi Town, Wuxing District, Huzhou City, Zhejiang Province
üè°Huzhou Giraffe Manor

.
"Huzhou Giraffe Manor" should be the first giraffe interactive manor in China. It was very famous on the major networks before, and I deliberately drove by myself in the summer.
.
The entire manor covers an area of 1,200 acres. Before moving in, park your self-driving car in the parking lot. The hotel will provide a tour bus transfer service. No matter where you are in the deep manor, you can always make a phone call.

.
The most attractive thing about Giraffe Manor is the breakfast. Guests staying at the hotel can have breakfast with giraffes. At breakfast time every day, the panoramic open floor-to-ceiling windows are all opened. Giraffes will stick out their heads to take pictures with hotel guests and feed them.

When checking in at the front desk, the front desk will have three time periods to choose from:
7 am to 8 pm. 8 am to 9 am. 9:00 to 10:00. The in-house guests in these three time periods have exclusive interactive experience in independent time periods.
.
The Giraffe Manor Park is very large, and there are many projects. If it is a parent-child activity or a group play, it is also very interesting.
The cute pet paradise has expanded by leaps and bounds. Bird wetland park, water park...
.
The buffet restaurant in the hotel manor is also quite rich for dinner. There are both Chinese and Western styles. You can choose according to different needs. Don't worry, you will not be able to eat three meals a day in it.

.
The three-storey single-family villa room booked in advance is moderately cost-effective, because it also includes breakfast, afternoon tea and dinner. Of course, because we have to stay in the whole manor for a long time, we also prepared a lot of snacks ourselves.

The overall layout of the room is reasonable, the sanitary condition is also very good, and the surrounding environment is also very good. The experience of staying in the whole room is very good, and the maintenance and usual maintenance are very good.
.
Personally, I highly recommend that you stay for one night. If you just go to the Internet celebrity to check in, you will lose a lot of experience. And his home stay experience is very good. recommend! !
